[![喷漆 30003001.png](https://patchwiki.biligame.com/images/klbq/1/1d/ofb3q34l4xz4e9es6lqo84sliki3eo0.png)](https://wiki.biligame.com/klbq/%E6%96%87%E4%BB%B6:%E5%96%B7%E6%BC%86_30003001.png "文件:喷漆 30003001.png")
